1b1(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA ga tA kA yA bA ka tsi ta ta gu h+ya a lang ka b+hA ha tanat+tA ra dza na ma/ bod skad du/ 
1b2(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba brgyan gyi bkod pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi
1b3(rgyud): rgyal po// bla ma dang 'byam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs kyi pad mo la gus par phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag
1b4(rgyud): gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs
1b5(rgyud): rdo rje ye shes rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs
2a1(rgyud): de ma mi shes phyag rgya chen de 'dam tshig gi sbyin gyis pa rnangs kyi rje chen po dang / de bzhin danan
2a2(rgyud): pathams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes chen po'i gcod pan gyi rtse mo'i gtsug phud kyi dbang bskur ba brnyes pa/ 
2a3(rgyud): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung rdo rje ye shes ting nge 'dzin chen po dang ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
2a4(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rje rje ye shes las sna tshogs pa chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku
2a5(rgyud): dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes chen po spro ba'i dam tshig gi gsang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung
2a6(rgyud): dang thugs rdo rje ma shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po'i dmachog gi khon nyid dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sru dngagasu
2b1(rgyud): dang thugs rdo rje ye shes gsung ba chen po'i seng po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi mnga' ba dag
2b2(rgyud): chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes kun du bzang po chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams
2b3(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes dpe med cing mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa nam mkha' lta bu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
2b4(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes rigs dang snying po dang / phyag rgya dang sngags dang rig pa gnyis su med par gyur pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
2b5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po la dga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs
2b6(rgyud): ba thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes lhag pa'i lha'i snying po mdzes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung
3a1(rgyud): dang thugs ye shes rgya mtsho chen po'i bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i snying po la nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi rdul dang mnyam
3a2(rgyud): pa'i rdo rje ye shes chen po 'ba' zhig dang / thabs gcig du bzhugs so// de'ang 'di la ste sgo mtha' yas pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje'i yum chen mo dang / 
3a3(rgyud): nam mkha'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / oM bo dza'i ske zhes bya ba'i yum chen mo dang / 'gyur ba med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i yum chen mo dang / 
3a4(rgyud): shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / gzhan yang ma lus cing lus pa med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul phra rab
3a5(rgyud): dang mnyam pa'i brtson 'grus dang ldan pa'i rdo rje btsun mo stong phrag brgya yang 'di lta ste/ mda'i mtshon cha'i lag ces rdo rje btsun me dang / 
3a6(rgyud): dbang phyug la lta ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang nye bar zhi ba'i bzhin ras zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / gyen du lta ba'i bzhin ras zhes
3a7(rgyud): bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / zla mtshan rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brda sprod pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dbang phyug gi 'ang 'dzis
3b1(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i de rje btsun mo dang / dmigs pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brang las skyes zhes bya ba'i di rje btsun mo ste/ de dag la sogs pa ni
3b2(rgyud): btsun mo rnams kyis yongs su bskor cing mdun du bdar ro// gzhan yang dpag tshun tu med pa'i rdo rje pho nya me chen mo rnams dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs
3b3(rgyud): te/ de yang 'di lta ste snying bskul bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po nya ma chen mo dang / gdug pa can thams cad 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po nyi mchen po dang / 
3b4(rgyud): rdorje su mnyes par rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje de nyam chen mo dang // khrag 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i ngorje po nya ma chen mo dang / thams nad 'phrog pa zhes bya bar
3b5(rgyud): rdo rje po nya ma chen mo dang / gzhan yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgyas pa'i rjerje zhes bya ba'i sgo srungs chen mo rnams dang yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di ltas
3b6(rgyud): rdo rje 'bebs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo bsrungs ma chen mo dang / dam tshig gsum ldan zhes bya ba'i rdo rje'i sgo bsrungs ma chen mo dang / 'jigs pa'i yan lag
3b7(rgyud): ces bya ba'i rdo rje sgo bsrungs ma chen mo dang / thog ma pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje chen mo dang / gdul dka' 'dul ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo bsrungs ma chen mo
4a1(rgyud): la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje blon mo chen mo dang / brtsigs shing rnam par 'gyur ba'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang yang thabs gcig
4a2(rgyud): ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ sku gsung thugs thams cad rdo rje 'chi ba ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jig pa'i me'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo rnam dang / brtsegs shing rnam
4a3(rgyud): par 'gyur ba'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jig rten gsum 'ching ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / bskal par gnas ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo la sogs pa'od/ 
4a4(rgyud): gzhan yang dpe med pa'i rdo rje rol mo pa rnams dang yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thamasacad kyi sku gsung thogs rdo rje dgas pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje
4a5(rgyud): rol pa dang / kun nas 'bebs pa zhes bya ba rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / 'jig rten gsum rab tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / rab tu dga' ba rdo rjes
4a6(rgyud): su 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / thams cad dga' bor byed pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo rnams la stsogs pa'o// gzhan yang na mkha'i khams thams cad rgyas par gang
4a7(rgyud): ba'i rdo rje'i yab rnams dang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste 'dod pa'i dbang phyug ces bya ba'i rdo rje'i ya ba chen po dang / mkha' 'gro'i dbang phyug rdo rje dang / dri'i dbang phyug dang / sdug
4a8(rgyud): po bkod pa dang / zla ba'i 'od dang / 'dun pa'i srel ba dang / skye ba yongs su dor ba dang / legs par sbyangs pa dang / 'dod pa'i rdo rje dang / bdud bskyed pa dang / 'dul ba byed pa dang / gdug pa/ 
4b1(rgyud): thams cad sel bar byed pa dang / de kho na nyid kyi 'gon po dang / gnas po dang / rtse ba can dang / chos 'chang dang / skyong ba po dang / sngob po dang / 'ching ba po dang / bskor ba po dang / de dag la sogs pa
4b2(rgyud): rdo rje yab rnams so// gzhan yang mtha' las 'das pa'i rdo rje pho nya mo 'jog pa'i bran po'i rdo rje'i tshigs dang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje rlung zhes bya ba dang / rdo rje me drang / rdo rje sa
4b3(rgyud): 'khrugs pa dang / rdo rje chu dang / gzhan yang rdo rje rgyal po chen po bzhi la 'di lta ste/ zhi bar byed pa dang / rgyas par byed la dang / dbang du byed pa dang / mi shes pa thams cad zad par byed
4b4(rgyud): pa de dag la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang mchog tu rgya chen porasangs rgyas kyi ye shes rab tu gnas pa'i mched pa dang ldan pa/ bcom ldan 'das ston pa rtag tu mchog
4b5(rgyud): gi mnga' bdag de// kun du bzang po'i sku yis ni// 'jig rten gsum gyi dkyil 'khor spros// bcom ldan 'das rdor 'dzin legs par bzhugs// gsang ba brgyan
4b6(rgyud): gyi sbyor bas so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bskyed pa'i yum gsang ba'i rdo rje 'dus par ma thob ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yab dang lhan cig tu rab tu dga' ba'i
4b7(rgyud): bde ba rdo rje su 'byung ste/ 'khor dang bcas pa rnams bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar lhags te/ rdo rje'i klu 'dis mngon par stod nas/ zhu ba zhus pa/ sangs rgyas kun khyod phyag 'tshal
4b8(rgyud): rdo rje 'byung ba khyod la 'dud// thugs kyi rin chen mchog khyod 'dud// chos kyi blo gros khyod la 'dud// chos rnams kun mchog khyod la 'dud// sna tshogs dgongs pa khyod la 'du de// dam
5a1(rgyud): tshig mchog khyod 'dud// rdo rje sems dpar phyag 'tshal 'dud// grags pa chen po bdag cag ni// mgon po khyod la zhu ba zhu// sangs rgyas thams cad skyed byed yum
5a2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor gyi ni dkyil 'khor mchog// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i yum rnams la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin
5a3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyis de skad ma zer cig/ 'jig rten thams cad la khyab pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po 'di ma 'ongs pa'i sems can rnams dang bar mi 'gyur zhing / rang gi sems yongs
5a4(rgyud): su sun 'byin pa des ma mthong ba'i chos la ma dad pas/ rang gi sems yang dag par sun phyung ste/ gnar med pa rnams su skyes nas bskal pa stong phrag mang po gnar med pa'i
5a5(rgyud): sdug bsngal rjes su 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de rgyalam na mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal las grol te/ mi rnams su skyes par gyur kyang rnam par 'gyur ba'i rang bzhin du 'gyur ro// 
5a6(rgyud): dede ngas pa rnams dang / blo gros chung ba rnams dang / khyi dang bya rog dang / byil dang / phag dang / stag dang / glang po che dang / seng ge'i nga ro 'dra ba dag du 'gyur ro// de dag rtam 'dre bar mi
5a7(rgyud): bya zhing / lta zhing bar mi bya'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bskyed pa'i yum de rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar sems can de rnams
5a8(rgyud): kyi gnar med pa'i sdug bsngal zad par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ gang gis 'di'i ming bzung nas yongs su zad par 'gyur ro// bsod nams de'i rgyus de'i las kyi
5b1(rgyud): bsgrib pa zad de/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi skal pa can du 'gyur ro// de nas de dag yid dga' ba skyes nas yang bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol rto/ 
5b2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das bstan du gsol// bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi rgyus dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyal po sems can thams cad la sman pa dang / bde ba'i phyir gang ma 'ongs pa'i sems
5b3(rgyud): can rnams kyis dran pa tsam gyis sangs rgyas kyi byang chub thob par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis kun du bzang po chen po 'phro ba gsal ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
5b4(rgyud): par bzhugs so// rang gi sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje rnams las de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i dam pa 'di bka' stsal pa// dkyil 'khor kun gyi yum gyur pa// 
5b5(rgyud): stong nyid ye shes nyid du bshing// ci zhig nga yis bstan par bya// rtog pa thams cad rnam par spangs/ sems can rnams la phan gzhed pas// gang zhig cung
5b6(rgyud): zad bstan par bya// stong nyid ye shes nyid du bshad// ci zhig nga yis bstan par bya// rtog pa thams cad rnam par spangs// sems can rnams la phan gzhed pas// gang zhig cung
5b7(rgyud): zed bstan par bya// de kun sgyu mas sgyu ma'o// 'gro ba sgyu ma lta bur shes// des na sgyu ma lta bu'i dkyil 'khor bya// nam mkha'i khrims kyis khyab pa'i// thams cad yum gyis yang dag 'khrug
5b8(rgyud): phyi rol yang ni rtag par bya// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor yum rnams kyi// dben zhing dga' ba'i gnas su ni// yid kyis legs par 'dus byas pa// nam mkha' la ni thig gis gdab// thog mar
6a1(rgyud): nga yis dam pa'o// de nas rnal 'byor chen po'i thig/ gsang ba'i yum gyi dkyil 'khor ro// mu khyud dag ni rnam bdun du// kun nas yongs su bskor bar bya// dbus kyi char ru
6a2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor ni// 'khor lo lta bu bri bar bya// kun nas brgyad gnyis mdzes pa ni// dkyil 'khor bzhi'i dbus su'o// 'khor lo'i lte ba'i dbus su ni// pad ma'i ze 'bru ldan pa bri// mtshams sam
6a3(rgyud): mtshams su 'dab ma ni// ji lta ba bzhin snyems bcas pas// srad bu lnga yis yang dag 'khrugs// slad bu bzhi yis nye bar spras// sgo bzhi dang ni yang dag ldan// rta babs seng ge dag gis brgyan// 
6a4(rgyud): gdugs dang rgyal mtshan pa ngan sogs// bla re steng du bris pa dang / de rin chen rdo rje pang ldan sngon// dpag bsam shing gi lcug mas khrug/ bum bzang rin chen ldan pa'i mchog/ brgyan 'dre
6a5(rgyud): glang po ldan pa ni// phyi rol gnas de legs par bri// rtog dang / mi rtog rnam spangs te// dkyil 'khor rgyal po'i dbus su ni// gsang ba brgyan gyi rdo rje byaH// mnyam par gzhag cing
6a6(rgyud): spro ba'i/ sems kyi bri ba nyid du bya// de nas lha mo zhal bzhi ma// shes rab pha rol phyin dge ma// phyag bzhi pa la spyan yangs me/ phyag gnyis kyis ni chos 'chad cing // zhi ba'i g.yas pa
6a7(rgyud): rdo rje ste// g.yon pa pad mas rnam par brgyan// dkar dang dmar po cher sngo ba// sngo sangs rin chen mchog mdzes 'od// gtsug na rin chen gtsug tor che// gtsug rgyan gcod pan dam pa can// bskal
6a8(rgyud): pa chen mo 'od ldan ma// brgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par klubs// gos kyis stod ni legs bsgribs pa// bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor 'dzum bcas shing // sna tshogs gos kyis legs brgyan pa// 
6b1(rgyud): dbu ma'i zhal ras gser gyi 'odo// zhabs gnyis dbus su 'khor lo ste// mdun na rin ri chen bdun gnas pa// pad ma mchog ldan seng ge'i khri// zla ba rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ba dan// nyi ma'i dkyil
6b2(rgyud): 'khor/ 'od 'phro ba// rgyal du nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// dpa'o de yis bri bar bya// dpa' mo sa mtha' yas pa'i zhal// mtshan nyid thams cad yang dag rdzogs// brgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// 
6b3(rgyud): phyag gis rdo rje pad ma 'chang // sna tshogs phyag rgyas phyag gzhan dkrigs// gtsug ldan dar gyi gcad pan can// u rgyan pad ma'i zhal ras ma// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dag la bzhugs/ 
6b4(rgyud): sna tshogs phyag de 'od nyi ma lta bu'i 'od// dpa'o'i rnal 'byor ldan pa'i// dpa' 'o des ni bri bar bya// rdo rje sems dpa' ra ba dag sgoms te// der ni bsnyems pas 'gro
6b5(rgyud): bar bya// dpa' bos lho ru bri bar bya// gshin rje'i 'dabam mdzes pa la// mchog sbyin nam mkha' dge ba marin chen khri legs par bzhugs// bzhin ras sngol
6b6(rgyud): spyan yangs ma// 'dzum bcas nor bu'i 'og bag can// 'gul rgyan rin chen 'phreng ba mchog/ rkang bdub gdu bu rin po che// yid bzhin nor bu lag pa can// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin dgongs
6b7(rgyud): mo// gcad phran gyis ni yang dag sbas// de nas blon ldan rab song ste// nub du yang ni de bzhin no// dpal dang ldan pas legs par bri// chu las skyes pa'i yid 'phrog ma// dmar
6b8(rgyud): mo'i gos 'dzin dag pa mo// gtsug na gcod pan gyis spras ma// skul brgyan sna tshogs lus can ma// dar dang rin chen gyis brlabs ma// pad ma 'byed pa'i sbyor ba'i// phyag gi lo 'dab
7a1(rgyud): dang ldan pas/ zla ba'i gdan la yang dag bzhugs// nyi ma du ma'i snang ba can// ji ltar rigs pa bri bar bya// de nas byang du phyin nas su// song ste dpa' bos bri bar bya// 
7a2(rgyud): me g.yo bzhin ras grags chen mya// mar gda' bar ba mtshungs pa'o// dkar po'i dar gyis yang dag brubs// gtsug na nor bu gcod pan da // gtsug rgyan sna tshogs dag gis sbas// 
7a3(rgyud): rdo rje dril bu la ga bkra ma// sna tshogs brgyan dang gos lA na mas// zla ba'i gdan la yang dag bzhugs ka 'od kyis btams pa'i dkyil 'khor 'chog/ de nas 'tshams kyi 'dab ma la
7a4(rgyud): me tog gdug pa dri lAn ma// rdo rje snang byed dge pa'i midi/ mchod pa sngags rigs pa yis bri// gzugs dang sgra dang ro dang reg/ rang gi bdag po'i phyogs su'o// 'dab mar
7a5(rgyud): thams cad nyid du gnas// zhi dang skyeg dang dbyangs chen mo/ gar gyi phyag rgya grags chen mo// sngags pas 'bad de bri bar bya// pad ma las skyes 'dab ma la// thams cad du ni
7a6(rgyud): grub pa gri// sgo rnams dag ni thams cad du// sgo skyong ba ni rnam bzhi dang // phyi rol tu mi rnams la sogs// ming ni yang dag bri bar bya// de nas khrus byas lugs byugs la/ 
7a7(rgyud): me tog gdugs sogs kyis gdugs te// sna tshogs gos ni rab gyon la// me tog 'phreng dang gos gyis brgyan// gtsug phud gcod pan dang ldan zhing // mdzes pa'i dor gyis yang dag
7a8(rgyud): klubs rdo rje dril bu lag pur ldan// sbyor ba bzang po'i rnam zhig gis// de nas thams cad dgug par bya// rdo rje ma mo dka' thub che// bzlog dang rnal 'byor ma'i phyag rgya yis// rdo rje
7b1(rgyud): sems dpa' bzlas nas su// rdo rje'i sbyor bas gar bya zhing // lan gsum du ni g.yas bskor bas// rdo rje ma mo'i dkyil 'khor rnams// dam tshig ldan pa thams cad byon// klu
7b2(rgyud): dbyangs kyi ni rgyal pos bskul// rang gi slob ma'i tshogs kyis ni// dris pa yis ni g.yas dang g.yon// 'gying ba dang ni 'dud par bya// 'dir gshegs 'dir gshegs sems
7b3(rgyud): can don mdzad brtson pa po// ser sna mi mnga' sangs rgyas tshogs mchog mtha' dag dang // bde gshegs dam pa'i yum 'gyur srid pa'i skyed pa po// pha rol don mdzad dus la de ring ba
7b4(rgyud): lags ces so// de nas de dag rang nyid kyis// rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul las byon// mtshan dag ni bzang po rnams so// dkyil 'khor dag du lta bar bya// rang ngam
7b5(rgyud): gzhan la 'bab sogs pa'i// mtshan ma ji ltar mthong bra na// de nas de dag rang nyid kyis// rdzu 'phrul rnam/ par 'phrul las byon// mtshan ma dag ni bzang po
7b6(rgyud): rnams// dkyil 'khor dag du lta bar bya// rang ngam gzhan la 'bab sogs pa'i// mtshan ma ji ltar mthong ba na / de tshe nges par ma mo no// bde gshegs thugs kyis
7b7(rgyud): dgongs par byon// de nas mchod yin zhabs gsil cho ga bzhin rab brtags te// de tshe 'babs pa'i sems can bso na mus ldan la bri bar bya// gal te de ni me smra ba na hUM
7b8(rgyud): gi yi ge dang / ldan pa'i klu dbyangs can gyis yongs su bskor ba'i nyid du bya// de nas shes rab ldan pas gzhug/ slob ma'i gtso bo thal sbyar te// mig la mig dar gyis g.yogs
8a1(rgyud): rang dga' bdag yin yang dag dga'// mamo thams cad sa dmigs te// der ni me tog dor bar bya// me tog glang la lhung gyur pa'i// ma mo de ni de yis 'grub// de nas
8a2(rgyud): go rims ji bzhin du// sgo skyong ba nas rtsams nas su// shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i bar// slob ma la ni bshad par bya// dam tshig thos par gyur nas su// sdom pa dag ni bzung bar bya// 
8a3(rgyud): ma mo'i sngags dang phyag rgya ni// 'gro mnyam par gzhag par bstan par bya// gzhan du slob dpon blo ngan ni// nges par dmyal bar 'dod par 'gyur// des kyang yang dag mi 'grub cing
8a4(rgyud): myur du dmyal bar 'gro bar 'gyur ba yin// gyegs dang / log par 'dren pa 'am// rims dang gdon dang dug sogs kyis// gdungs te nad kyis rgyun du ni// 'chi ba ru
8a5(rgyud): yang 'gyur ba yin// rdo rje slob dpon smad pa can// rtag tu dmyal ba nyid du ni// rab tu rmongs pa'i slob ma 'argya/ mkha' las rdo rje ji bzhin no// des bu ke dam tshig ni/ 
8a6(rgyud): khyod kyis rtag tu bsrung bar byos// ma mo kun gyi sdom pa ni// theg pa chen po'i tsho gas gnas te// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs te// rdo rje
8a7(rgyud): 'dzin pa thams cad kyi yum rnams kyi/ dam tshig bka' stsal pa/ rin chen sems kyi dam tshig gis// rnam pa gsum ni sbyang bar bya/ thog mtha' bar gyi sbyor bya yis// chung 'bring mchog
8a8(rgyud): gi dbye ba yis// de 'dra'i dam tshig yongs dag pa// sangs rgyas kun gyis bka' stsal to// ji sems pa ni sbyangs kyi bar// 'bad pa yis ni bsgom par bya// bud med thams cad mthong ba ma
8b1(rgyud): lan gsum du ni bskor nas kyang // spyi bos phyag ni byas nas su// lan gsum bar du gsol ba bdang // bdag gi ma khyod bu yin te// ji srid byang chub thob par du// byang chub yan lag
8b2(rgyud): nu ma las// byung ba'i rang gi 'o mas skyongs// de nas sbyor ldan rab gang ba'i// dbang skur ba ni sbyin par bya// gser la sogs pa'i bum pa ru// dri'i chus ni yongs bkang la// dar dang
8b3(rgyud): ras gsogs kyis g.yogs te// me tog chun pos mgul brgyan nas// rin chen sman gyis bkang ba'i// gcig lhag bcu drug bzang po la// ma mo'i snying po nyid kyis ni// brgya
8b4(rgyud): brtsa brgyad du bzlas pa yis// sngags shes pas ni dbang bskur ro// slob ma zhi ba bzang po yis// thog mar zhu ba byas nas ni// zhabs gnyis la ni 'gos btud nas/ 
8b5(rgyud): bdag ni che ge mo rdo rje che// byang chub sems ni rnam bsgom pa'o// slob dpon zhabs kyi chu skyes la// dbang bskur/ phyir ni zhu ba bgyid// skal pa chen po bdag la stsol/ 
8b6(rgyud): slob dpon mchog tu rmad byung ba// dbang bskur rgyal ba thams cad kyis// sangs rgyas byang chub rab bsgrub pa/ de ni bdag gis sems can rnams// don gyi dam pa
8b7(rgyud): bdag gis bgyi// sangs rgyas kun gyis don bgyid pa// rtul shugs bzang po khyod kyi drin// de nas dbang skur sbyor ba yis// rdo rje sems dpa'i go 'phang gnas// slob ma 'ang
8b8(rgyud): ye shes rdo rje yi// go 'phang la ni gzhag nas su// bum po bzang po gcig gam ni// yang na bcu drug dag gam ni// lnga 'am yang na bcu yis ni// dkyil 'khor du ni dbang bskur ma/ 
9a1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor gyi ni 'dun du ni// dkyil 'khor pad ma bri bar bya// pad ma lo ma brgyad pa las// ge sar lte ba ldan pa dri// de'i dbus su rdo rje bri// sna tshogs rdo rje 'od zer 'phreng / 
9a2(rgyud): de'i mdun du 'khor lo bri// chen po rin chen bdun gyis bskor// lho'i phyogs su rin po che// nu du pad ma nyid yin te// byang chub du ral gri chen po'o// 'bar ba'i phreng 'khrugs 'od zer
9a3(rgyud): can// gra'i phyogs ni thams cad du// me tog gdug pa dri zhim pa// 'od ldan pa ni skal ba che// skyo dang sgo ru bzhi nyid do// phyi rol du'ang mi 'chi kun// gcig nas gcig du rgyal
9a4(rgyud): sgrogs pa// gang byed bcer bu'i cha lugs te// ming nga thos pa dang ldan pa'o// dkyil 'khor de'i dbus su ni/ slob ma snyems dang bcas pa gzhag/ chos kyi rang bzhin
9a5(rgyud): gtam spyod de// der khyod ni rigs su skyes// 'khor/ lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po che// rtag pa dam pa'i dbang phyug pa// thabs dang shes rab ldan pa'i dpal// dag
9a6(rgyud): pa'i dbang phyug kun gyi rgyal// rdo rje pad ma lag byin te// gnang ba bzang po rab tu sbyin// bu yis bya ba chen po gyis// sangs rgyas kun gyi go 'phang gnas// der ni sbyor ba 'ongs nas
9a7(rgyud): su// gsang ba'i sdom pa sbyin par bya// 'di ni mchog tu dga' ba ste// yum rnams rab tu rmad du byung ba'o// dus su 'dod pa nyid du gyis// dam tshig mchog du gyur pa'o// brtul shugs
9a8(rgyud): bzang pos ci 'byor pas// de nas yon ni phul nas su// slob dpon gyi ni zhabs la btud// ma dang chung ma bu mo dang // sring mo sring mo'i bu mo dang // bu rnams dang ni bdag nyid dang // / 
9b1(rgyud): rgyal po longs spyod gter dang ni// nor dang 'bru dang grong shing rta// glang po rta dang ba grang sogs// ma he dang ni ma he mo// gzhan dang gzhan yang ci 'dod pa// bla ma la ni chen pos dbul/ 
9b2(rgyud): bya dang mi bya rdzas kyi mchog/ thams cad kyang ni dbul bar bya// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnams la// rgyan 'phreng rnams dang gzhan gang dang // skyeg dang rtse 'jo dga' ba dang // rab
9b3(rgyud): tu dga' ba'i bde tshe na dang // bza' btung bca' ba la sogs pa// rnam pa du ma thams cad kyis// mchod nas gshegs su gsol bar bya// sems can kun gyi don dang ni// bdag
9b4(rgyud): gau yang ni ches cher mdzad// bder gshegs gang du gshegs pa der// ma mo thams cad gshegs su gsol// shes rab ldan pas yon phul te// slob ma mchog dang
9b5(rgyud): bcas pa yis// gar byas lag pa mgor gzhagaste// rims kyis 'gyed dang 'dud par// de nas bzang po rnam mnyes te// thams cad bsgrub par byed pa'i
9b6(rgyud): mchog/ bdag gi bskal bzang bsal nas kyang // rang gi sras kyi gnas su gshegs// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje ye shes yum chen mo rnams kyi phyag rgya
9b7(rgyud): chen po'i ye shes kyi 'khor lo yongs su rdzog s+ho// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum// bcom ldan 'das ma rnams kyis yang gsang ba 'dus pa las
9b8(rgyud): byung ba/ rang rang gi bsgrub pa'i thangs rgyas po bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad zhus so// shes rab ye shes mchog bsgrub pa'i// sems dpa' chen pos gsung du gsol// thabs kyis
10a1(rgyud): sems can thams cad kun// sangs rgyas byang chub 'bras thob pa// rdo rje ye shes mchog gyur pa// rdo rje sku ste rdo rje mchog/ dngos grub kun gyi bde ster ba// rdo rje chen pos// 
10a2(rgyud): gsung du gsol// thugs kyi rin chen ldan pa'i mchog/ gzi brjid rdo rje snang ba can// sems can rnams kyi rdzi 'phrul dang // bsgrub pa'i yon tan 'byung gnas gsungs// 
10a3(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi rnal 'byor che// dpa' bo'i sbyor bas rab gnas pa'i// dpa'o chen pos bshad du gsol// las kun gyi ni 'bras ba rnyes pas// sna tshogs mkhyen pa dbang phyu/ 
10a4(rgyud): che// sems can rnams kyi yab chen po// sna tshogs dam dpas bshad du gsol/ las kun gyi ni 'bras ba zhes/ byaso// de nas bcom ldan 'das rtag pa'i rgyal/ 
10a5(rgyud): dam pa'i dbang phyug kun mkhyen pas// gsung mchog nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa'o// zab mo'i ni chos ba/ stsol 'di ni bsgrub po gang yang med// dngos grub
10a6(rgyud): bam ni sgrub thabs kyang // thams cad rnam par rtog las byung // rnam rtog kyang ni rigs ma yin// bdag dang sangs rgyas rnams kyang med// khyod rnams med cing chos nyid med
10a7(rgyud): sbyor ba med cing sems can med// de bzhin pha ma yang med// byed pa med cing skyong ba med// 'bras bu med cing rgyu yod min// long spyod med cing zab mo med// shes med shes pa
10a8(rgyud): bo yang med// rnam shes med cing shes bya med// brdzun min bden pa'ang ma yin pa// des na snang ba thams cad ni// sgyu ma lta bu nyid las byung // de ltar chos rnams rnam rig na
10b1(rgyud): grol nas gos par mi 'gyur te// dngos grub chen po 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub bde chen po// zab mo'i chos ni thos pa na// mkhas pa gang zhig drung gyur na/ 
10b2(rgyud): snying po phyag rgya sngags rig rnams// gdon mi za bar 'grub par 'gyur// sbyor ba 'di ni bcom ldan gsungs// thams cad bye dag par byed pa'i mchog/ gsang ba'i rgyan
10b3(rgyud): legs bzhugs nas// sems can rnams la brtan pa'o// de nas yum rnams tshim 'gyur te// rang byung ba la zhu ba zhus// sgrub pa'i sgrub thubs rab sbyar ba// mnga' bdug
10b4(rgyud): rnal 'byor rnams kyis gsungs// de nas yang bcom de ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyiyum las kyi dam tshig 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i
10b5(rgyud): nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// nam mkha'i dkyil 'khorabasgom par bya// de'i steng du mnyam gzhag pas/ 
10b6(rgyud): nam mkha'i mtha' las khyab pa'i// phyogs kun du ni rab 'phro ba'i// de'i steng du gzi brjid che// dus mda'i me dong 'tshungs 'dra ba// de'i steng du sa chen po// gser
10b7(rgyud): ri bo dang mtshungs pa// de'i steng du tshur shes bya// zla ba gang ba kha 'dra ba// sngags pa yis ni cho ga bsam// rin chen bzhi ni rang bzhin bzang // stong phrag brgya bcu rtsa bzhi
10b8(rgyud): dpag tshad kyis ni tshad tsam pa// gru bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa// rta babs bzhi'i rtse mo can// ri bo dag ni bcog brgyad pa// dbus su rdo rje'i ri bo mchog/ de'i steng du rdo rje che// 
11a1(rgyud): kun du tshogs pas yongs su bskor// sngo sangs mA ra ka ta 'dra// sna tshogs 'od kyis yang dag 'khrugs// de'i steng du rdo rje rje// rtse mo lnga pa rnam par bsam// kar po shel dang
11a2(rgyud): 'dra ba po// 'od zer lnga yis rnam par spras// de'i steng du rin po che// chu skyes sngon po'i 'dab 'dra ba// sna tshogs 'od zer stong gi 'phreng // phyogs bcu nam mkha' khyab pa po// de'i gtsug
11a3(rgyud): tu pad ma che// nam mkha' khyab pa'i ni mchog/ lo ma stong phrag du ma can// lte ba dang ni ze 'brus dkrigs// de'i mdun du nyi ma che// 'od zer stong phrag du ma can// de'i steng du zla ba che/ 
11a4(rgyud): dkar po'i 'od zer 'bar bas dkrigs// nam mkha'i khams ni kun gang ba'i// gzi brjid dkar dang 'phro ba po// de'i dbus su ma mo bri// dus gsum gzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas
11a5(rgyud): kyang // yongs su dag pa mkha' 'dra ma// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'phro ba mo/ phyag gnyis ma la thugs zhig na/ bsam gtan spyan sngar bsam gtan yid// bsam gtan
11a6(rgyud): mchog gi phyag rgya'i// sor mo bzhon nu rab gzhag pa// dkar po'i gos 'dzin mdzes pa'o// dkar po yis ni brgyan gyis brgyan// ral ba'i thor tshugs gcod pan bzang // gtsug gi nor
11a7(rgyud): bus 'od ldan pa// ye shes bdan la mnyam par bzhugs// ba sku rnams kyi rtse phug nas// rgyal ba'i bar du rab 'phros te// byang chub pha rol son pa mdzad// de'i thugs kar rnam bsams/ 
11a8(rgyud): pa// yi ge mchog du mi 'gyur ba// yi ge rnams kyis mnga' bdag dkrigs// thams cad du ni legs 'phro ba// sangs rgyas rnams ni 'dun gnas pa// rab tu thal mo sbyar ba'o// 
11b1(rgyud): de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' rnams// rigs sngags khro bo'i tshigs kyang ni// chos nyan pa'i tshul du yang // dkyil 'khor du ni bzhug par bya// ske'i phyogs ni thams cad du// sgo
11b2(rgyud): ba ni bzhi rnams so// ston pa la sogs ci rigs par// bcu drug po'ang gzhag par bya// me tog bdug pa mer me che// ji ltar ba bzhin bzhag par bya// lA klu de bzhin gnod sbyin dang // 
11b3(rgyud): dri za lha min dmyal las byung // 'di rnams thams cad ldan pa la// kun nas yongs gzhag par bya// de nas me tog 'phreng ldan 'jug/ dri dang me tog yang dag ldan// goso kar 'dzin
11b4(rgyud): pa dpal dang ldan// brgyan rnams kun gyis rnam parabargyan// shes rab 'phro dang lhan cig du// rdo rje sems dpa' rjes dran pas// bdag dag pas ni dag par
11b5(rgyud): bya// shes rab sbyor bas gang gnas pas// sgo'i drung du legs 'khod la// klu 'di yis ni spyan drang bya// thugs rje mnga' ba chos kyi dbang phyug sangs rgyas yum
11b6(rgyud): rung gi yab kyi tshogs dang bca smras dang bcas te byon// skyon cig smyon cig lha dang srin por bcas mched pa'i// 'jig rten dbang phyug yang dag byang chub thugs mnga' ba// skyon gyig
11b7(rgyud): skyon cig thugs rje'i bdag nyid 'jig rten gnyen// chos kyi yi ge bde bar gshegs pas rjes bskos pa// mkha' ltar yongs dag dri med dam bcas dran par mdzad// mo mo
11b8(rgyud): rnams kyi mchog gi klus bskul byon par 'gyur// de nas bcom ldan 'das ma byon par mthong nas// rang gi me tog gi snyim pa dang mchod yon dang zhabs gsil dbul bar bya'o// 
12a1(rgyud): oM bdag gi mchod yon zhabs gsil 'di// ni b+hi bar ni gnyis su gsol// de nas de dang ldan cig tu/ 'dres par du ni gyur b+har bsam// oM barba ta thAk+Sh+ma tA Thadz+dza
12a2(rgyud): ny+dzanas ma yi ston// de nas 'di las btsun par bya ste// mA~M ra ta nAg tu tsam swA m+b+ha mem sa te/ de nas 'dis mnyes par bya// oM sarbata ga ta ma na san du sa mam
12a3(rgyud): mi baM hUM/ e ha hi ya dzA/ A yA hi dza/ de nas dpag tu med pa'i ngo mtshar chen po lta ba'i phyir/ oM sar+b+ba oM gsun da ri ma hA b+ha gi 'das le s+phA ra sma ra swa ra swa ra/ sarba a g+ha a
12a4(rgyud): gub ma hA sa mu tra hUM hUM gnyis oM TI/ 'di yis ma mo bskul nas su// sangs rgyas sprin ni 'od po che// dkyil 'khor sa la spro bar bya// de nas gsang sngags 'di yis ni
12a5(rgyud): sngags te me tog der bar bya// oM sarba a gsun/ da ro ti tsha daM ku su ma a na dza li ma hUM/ aM/ de nas/ ji ltar gzhed pa bzhin du/ dkyil 'khor gyi bum pa rnams
12a6(rgyud): la/ rigs sngags 'dis ji ltar bshad pa ltar legs par byin gyis rlabs la rang gi dbang bskur rang gi snying rang gis blang bar bya'o// de nas las cad kyi nus pa dang ldan
12a7(rgyud): ba dang / dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas me tog la sogs dang // bza' dang btung dang ro dag gis// mchod la sngon gyi rim pa bzhin// slob ma'i rgyal po
12a8(rgyud): bzhug par bya// 'khor lo sbyar ba'i rim pa yi// sbyor ba yis ni dbang bskur ro// rdo rje rin chen de bzhin pad// las kyi rdo rje de bzhin no// zhags pa lugs kyu dril bu dang / 
12b1(rgyud): spogs dang rnga yab dang ni gdugs// ral gri mag sngan thur ma dang // rgyal po'i nye bar spyod ma dang // de la brgyan rnams stan nas su// dkyil 'khor der ni dbang bskur ro// rgyal
12b2(rgyud): bu'i yum gyi dbang bskur bas// las kun byed par rab tu bshad// dam tshig gam ni sdom pa yang // rang gi slob ma nyan du bzhug/ zhi ba dang ni rgyas pa'i las// dbang dang
12b3(rgyud): drag shul spyod pa ni// legs par rnam par dag sems kyis// ci 'dod par ni bya ba byos// las rnams kyi ni 'bras bu yang // sbyor 'di yis 'grub par 'gyur// de nas
12b4(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' chen pos slar yang las dam pa rgyas par bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas 'di skad ces bka'
12b5(rgyud): sprul to// ji ltar gzugs kyi snod byas nas// dkyil 'khor 'di ni dbus su gzhag// zho dang mar gsar 'o ma ni// tsan dan dmar po dang bsres te// ga bur dang ni
12b6(rgyud): ldan byas la// yid la byed pas bzlas te 'grub// zla ba nyi ma bzas bzung tshe// sbyor ba bzang po'i rnam gzhag bya// thog mar me ni slar byas nas// 'bad pa yis ni rlung gis b+h+yas
12b7(rgyud): gser gyi snod du bsdu bar bya// ba ru na'i khubs spang // nyi ma dang ni zla ba la// slar yang rdzas de bskum par bya// de nas de ru lha mo'i// khrag dang sa bon blugs par bya// de yis
12b8(rgyud): myur du rdzas dag ni// 'grub par 'gyur te the tshom med// grub nas thob mar lha mo la// cung zad tsam cig sbyin par bya// de bzhin du ni slob dpon la// skal ba gnyis 'gyur dbul bar
13a1(rgyud): bya de nas grub pa gzhan rnams dang // rang gis thog mar skal pa sbyin// de nas byin rlabs sbyor ba yis// phyag rgya dang ni lhan cig tu// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting 'dzin gyis
13a2(rgyud): zas kyi sa bon dang ni bza'// skad de la gzugs rjes te// rdo rje sems dpa' lta bur 'gyur// gang dang gang gis gzugs rnams su// bsgrub pa 'dod pa'i sngags pa yis// de'i
13a3(rgyud): dang de'i bsam gtan gyis// blo gros gtan pas bza' bar bya// de dang de'i gzugs su ni// gdon mi za bar rje bar 'gyur// gzhan pa yi ni rdzas dag dang // 'di nyid kyis ni bsgrub
13a4(rgyud): bar bya// mag sman gyis ni mig byugs pas// khor yug du ni mi snang 'gro// snying la ldong ros gyis byugs nas// yid kyi spyod yul nyid du 'gro// ba ba la yis ni
13a5(rgyud): lus byugs na// mkha' la nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur/ mig sman nag po blangs nas su// nag po'i phyogs la bza' bar bya// de'i gshang ba'i mar khu las/ 
13a6(rgyud): dud pa mkhas pas bsgrub par bya// de yis mig la byugs na ni// mkha' la nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas kyis kyang mi gzigs shing // stobs ni dpal ldan
13a7(rgyud): mtshon// nyid 'gyur rgo dang 'chi ba med// mig sman dang ni ba lang mar// ma h+ye dang ni ra nyid dang // ma'i mig smig nyid dag ni// mkhas pa yis ni blangs nas ni/ 
13a8(rgyud): sngags pas bzung ste btse bar bya// mig sman chen po mchog du bzang // 'di yis mig la byugs na ni// grub pa yid du 'ong bar 'gyur// mi snang grub pa thams cad kyi
13b1(rgyud): gros chen po rgyal bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas kyis sa chen po// nges par thob 'gyur gzhan du min// rdzas kyi gnas skabs le'u 'di// mtshungs med chungs med po nye bar bsha
13b2(rgyud): gos dang gdugs dang gsogs ral gri dang // mtshon chad ma pa bsgrub par bya// snying po snying khar byas nas nas ni// goms na myur du 'grub par 'gyur// rdo rje sems
13b3(rgyud): dpa' rgyal po chos// pad ma'i sems dpa' bzhin ras mchog/ de'i zhal du byas nas su// de dang ldan par sgom par bya// mnga' bdag gar gyi dbang phyug ltar// skad cig
13b4(rgyud): de la de 'gyur ro// de nyid kyi ni spyi bo'i char// mchog/ gi dam pa bsam gtan bya// skad cig de la mchod pa// che'i// sangs rgyas su ni de 'gyur ro// de'i spyi gtsug nyid
13b5(rgyud): du ni// sna tshogs rdo rje sgom paro bya// de ni kun gyi rgyal dbang po// las kun byed pa'i don grub 'gyur/ rdo rdza snying khar bsam par bya// de'i dbus su snying po lnga
13b6(rgyud): de nas rdo rje rig pa 'dzin// mnga' bdag rdo rje'i dbang po 'grub// rin chen chen po che brgyad pa// snying kha ru ni mkhas pas sgom// der ni snying po bsams pa yis// rin chen rig
13b7(rgyud): pa 'dzin par 'gyur// pad ma chen po 'dab brgya pa// yid la bsgoms pas skad cig la// pad ma che ldan mnga' bdag gi// pad ma'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// de la sogs
13b8(rgyud): pa mtha' yas pa// ji lta'i sbyor ba'i cho ga yis// mchog dang dman pa 'bring po'i// dngos grub dam pa bsgrub par bya// snying kar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor bsam// yi ge dam
14a1(rgyud): po sgom par bya// ji ltar sbyor bas dkyil 'khor gyis// thams cad bdag du bsgom par bya// de las langs de bdag zhi bas// b+hU 'od kha bltar gsil ba'i// 'od zer
14a2(rgyud): sprin gyis cher gtams pa// sgrub bya'i spyi bor gnag par bya// skad cig de la gdug par bya// gzha' dang dug sogs rab 'phrog cig/ nyi ma gcig gam bdun du ni// bsgrub bya ni
14a3(rgyud): 'gyur gzhan du min// rin chen dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// snying po'i mchog ni bsgom par bya// de las langs te bdag zhi bas// 'od zer ser po'i 'phreng 'dzes pa// boskems pas
14a4(rgyud): de ni rgyas par byed// pad ma'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas dpar// mnyam par gzhag pas lha mo bsam// dpa po'i rang bzhin 'bar dag pa// bsgrub bya sems la 'gro bar
14a5(rgyud): bya// slar yang bsrud pa'i sbyor ba yis// rang gi lus bzhug par bya// 'khor lo sgyur ba lta bu yang // de nas ci nas dbang du 'gro// las kyi dkyil 'khor rab
14a6(rgyud): gnas par// de'i dbus su yi ge ni// mar dkar 'od 'dra sgom par bya// 'od zer smin gyis yang dag 'khrugs/ mkhas pa yis ni snying kar bsam// bsgrub bya la ni snying po
14a7(rgyud): 'od// snyoms pa'i spyad cig de la 'bab// rdo rje gar gyis gar byed cing // phyag rgya sbyor ba'i rnal 'byor dang // rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sbyor ba'i// phyag rgyas thams cad ston par
14a8(rgyud): 'gyur// 'das dang ma 'ongs ci 'dod dag mi dge/ lce rkyang bas ni smra bar byed// 'dod dang mi 'dod dge mi dge// rdo rje ngadag gis smra bar 'gyur// yang na legs par sbyar ba 'am/ 
14b1(rgyud): grong gi tha mar skad dag gis// 'dod dang mi 'dod dge mi dge// 'tsho ba 'am ni 'chi ba dang // nyams dang mi nyams rang bzhin gyi// de dag thams cad de yis smra// de las gzhan du de mi smra// / 
14b2(rgyud): 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje can// dbang bdag rdo rje'i dbyangs kyis gsungs// khros te lce la rtser sgoms nas ni// lha mo yi ni snying po mchog// lcags kyu'i rnam pa spros nas su// 
14b3(rgyud): phyag rgya dang ni phyag rgya'i lan// rlung la gzhag ste skad gcig la// khrag rnams thams cad dgug par bya// char rgyun 'bab pa'i sbyor ba yis// rang gi kha ru dbab par bya// de ni 'thungs
14b4(rgyud): pas sngags shes te// mnga' bdag rdo rje 'dzin 'gyur// nam mkha' kun du sbyor dpal ldan// nyi ma'i snang ba la dbur 'gyur// 'di nyid kyi ni rnal 'byor byos// 'o ma zho dang
14b5(rgyud): mar bzang po// mer khu chu dang me tog kun// rlung gis/ dgug pa nyid du bya// zhags pas 'grin pa bcings/ byas te// lcags kyu yis ni snying kha nas// rlung gis
14b6(rgyud): kun nas bteg nas su// lha mo de bzhin gnod sbyin mo// ma mo de bzhin lha mon mo// brgyad rgyu kho na bzlas pas ni// bud med tshul du dgug par bya// bsgrub byed bsgrub byed ming

14b8(rgyud): ma mchog/ khro bo dang ni yang dag ldan// bsal byed kyis ni bsal byas pas// las rnams dag ni thams cad bya// dur khrod ro ni ma nyams pa// mar ngo'i rgyad la sdus nas/ 
15a1(rgyud): byang du phyogs te gzhag par bya// de'i khar ni mnyam gzhag pasan/ gsang sngags legs par bzlas nas su// rdzas kyi dam pa ci rigs pa// bab la mig sman rdo rdung
15a2(rgyud): dang // ldong ris drong yang yang na btsug/ kar ci sol pa nyid dang ni// gur gus dang ni mye smos sas// dU Na shu dag gla bur dang // tsan dan de bzhin a ka ru// sha dang khrig ni cing
15a3(rgyud): dang ni// de bzhin sor mo'i gdu bu ni// rnal 'byor ldan pas gzhag nas kyang // de'i ngang la sdad la zla// nyi ma sha rare nas de blangs nas// grub pa'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur/

15b2(rgyud): 'dren pa'o// ga khur nyid ni zos pa yis// gzhan du'ang de'i dbang du 'gyur// rig pa chen mo yi ge bzhi// mnyam par sbyor bzhug pa'i sbyor ba yis// 'khrug pa dang ni spel nas su//

16b6(rgyud): nor 'dzin sangs rgyas yum la'o// phyogs bzhi dag du phur bus gdab // de nas gnas rnams bskrad par bya// de nas mtshan ni bcing bar bya// mnyam par gzhag ste skor bar byed
16b7(rgyud): sbyor ba shes pas sngags 'di yis// de nas rdzas rnams gdon par bya// oM ba su d+ha sarba thA sa d+ha ni sA d+ha ya sA d+ha ye/ u pA ra u dA ra/ ra kA rak+Sha/ sarba rA ni tsa yaM/ tr-i tr-i tsa tsa Ta Ta ha ha swa hA/

17a1(rgyud): ni nor 'dzin la'o// sdug bsngal can la cha gcig go// grogs rnams dag ni de bzhin mtshungs// lhag ma rnams ni rigs pas spyad// dkon mchog gsum la legs mchod

20b4(rgyud): dkyil 'khor sbyor bas bsgom pa dang // kun 'da' dkar po zla ba 'dra// 'od zer dkar pos mdzes pa po// skye bo nad pa 'chi ka mo// de'i lus la gzhug par bya// de nas de'i lus
20b5(rgyud): la bzhug par bya// de nas de ni stobs ldan 'gyur// brgyad gnyis pa'i khang tshor snang // nad rnams kun la so rnam par grol// rga dang 'chi ba rnams par spangs// snyan chos
20b6(rgyud): kun gyi don rig cing // shes rab dran pa mchog dang ldan// de bzhin rang bzhin rnal 'byor pa// na mkha' la yang yang dag bsgom// mdzes pa rin chen sna tshogs pa'i
20b7(rgyud): thams cad ni char 'bab pa// 'di yis 'phongs pa rnam par 'phrog/ 'phongs pa rnams la rnam par rab tu rtag/ mthe bo che'i tshad tsam pa'i// nor rgyun ma'i rnam pa bya// lha mo la ni

21a1(rgyud): nyin par la// mchod pa chen po byas nas su// mkhas pas mtshan mo thog thag bzlas// de nas dga' bas gzugs rnyan de// gdon mi za bar 'bar bar 'gyur// de nas

22a1(rgyud): po can khrag gis gang ba'i thod pa dang // phyag rgya bzang pos phyag mtshan pa'o// de'i phyir ru lha rnams ni// snying khar rab sbyar yid dang ba// thams cad du ni yongasu gzhag/

22b7(rgyud): cad 'gugs pa'i dam pa yis// mkha' gdong ma yis thams cad du// rin po che'i tshogs 'byung ngo // pad ma'i zhal gyi sbyor ba yis// chang gi dam pa bzung bar bya// ma bcom ma'i sbyor ba

23a1(rgyud): pa'i las rnams dang // ma bshad pa'i las rnams dang // ma gshad pa'ang ci 'dod pa// bzlas pa tsam gyis kun bya ste// thams cad du ni the tsom med// dur khrod kyi ni

26b8(rgyud): mchod pa chen po kye// cha lugs rnam pa du mas 'gro kun 'dul mdzad kun gyis dam pa kye// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol ba btab cing bskal
27a1(rgyud): pa'i tshig nyid kyi thugs la gzhag nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo sgyur chen po rab tu bsim pa/ bde ba longs spyod pa rnam par sgyings pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting / 
27a2(rgyud): nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs te dbang bskur nas/ bde ba chen po 'khor lo sgyur ba la rab tu gnas/ sku dang gsung dang thugs
27a3(rgyud): rdo rje rnams las rab tu byung ngo // dkyil 'khor snga ma bzhin bris la// de'i lte bar 'di dgod do// rdo rje chen po gsal ldan pa// 'dod pa'i dbang phyug dag dang ldan// de bzhin gshegs
27a4(rgyud): pa kun gyi yab// kun gyi thog mtha' rang 'byung ba// de la sog/ pa'i rim pa yis// thams cad kun du brtags pa bya// dpad ma'i 'khor lo'i rtsibs la ni// rang gi chos dang rab
27a5(rgyud): tu spel// ma mo rnams ni thams cad kyi// mchod pa la sogs rab tu rtag/ sgo ru skyo ba yongs su rtag/ sgo'i phyisgo skyong ba// btsun mo lhan cig spyod bcas pa'i// kun
27a6(rgyud): nas lha rnams gzhag par bya// de nas rang gi sa bon gyis// klu dang gnod sbyin 'phar ma gzhag/ dri za rnams dang mo 'am ci// lha mo ni mkhas lding de bzhin no// 'jig rten skyong ba thas
27a7(rgyud): cad ni// sgo ru gnyis gnyis rtag par bya// gdon dang dug dang rims dang nad// yi dgas sha za srin po dang // dmyal ba brgyad po phyogs brgyad kyi// 'khor lo'i phyi ru gzhog par
27a8(rgyud): bya // de nas 'khor lo'i mu khyud bri// chen po rin chen bdun rang bzhin// de'i sgo ru bri bar bya// shar du 'dod chags skye gnas lag// zhe sdang drag po lus gnag pa// byang du
27b1(rgyud): legs par bri bar bya// lho ru nga rgyal nyid yin no// sog le dang ni gos nag po// de bzhin dbyug gu 'jigs chen po// 'di rnams phyag brgyar brtags pa'o// de nas ji lta bzhin du 'jug/ 
27b2(rgyud): de nas gsang ba rdo rje'i phyag rgya nges par bcings pa'i lag par gyur pas// rang gi dam tshig gi rjes su dran pas phyag rgya de nyid kyis 'gugs pa'i rnam par dang // rdo rje'i klu 'dis bskul
27b3(rgyud): te/ dkyil 'khor thams cad spyan drang bar bya ste// 'dir gshegs 'dir gshegs sangs rgyas zhalnga ras sangs rgyas dpa'// bde bar gshegs pa yum dang bcas pa mtha' dag gis
27b4(rgyud): bskor te/ 'dir gshegs 'dir gshegs pad ma'i spyan rna ras bad las 'khrungs// dam tshig rnams kyis dApa'o// dam pa'i phyag/ klu dbyangs rgyal po 'di yis ni// rdo rje'i
27b5(rgyud): glo gros nges par bskul// byon gyur song shig song shig ces/ 'khod cig 'khod tsag mkhod par bya// tsham zhing tsham/ la rab tu tshim// zhugs cig zhugs 'jug par bya// bag kye
27b6(rgyud): zhes brjod bskul ba yis// sa la gnas kun rab tu 'bebs// de nas me tog dor bar bya// bcom ldan 'das bde bar gzhes su gsol// lha dbang gang la lhung 'gyur bzung // de'i bsgrub thabs
27b7(rgyud): rtsam par bya// yang na yid la gang 'dod pa// bsgrub byed bsgrub po dam pas sgrub// de nyid la ni dbang skur ba// rnal 'byor pa ni mkhas pas blang // de nis slob ma bzhug par bya// brgyan nas
27b8(rgyud): kun gyis rnam par brgyan// dar sogs pas gdong g.yo ge taM/ phyag rgya bcangs pa'i lag bzang pos// de bzhin du ni me tog dor// sa mo ya so bdag gas brjod// me tog gang la lcang gyur pad de'i
27'a1(rgyud): bcu mu med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad khyab pa'i rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams bkang ste// na mkha'i khams na gnas pa thams cad til gi gang bu ltar 'dzam bu'i gling nas 'khyod par
27'a2(rgyud): gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje thogs rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug gis bkug cing bcug te/ bcing nas dbang du mdzad de/ de nyid thugs kar rab tu bzhag par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan
27'a3(rgyud): 'dis rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbangade phyug chen pos gnyis su med pa'i sbyor bas byin gyis rlabs te/ sngags 'dis rang gi sems so sor rtogs par mdzad do// oM tsa~M d+ha pra ti bi d+h+r-i ka ro mang/ 
27'a4(rgyud): thogs nyid la/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs kar long spyod rdzogs po dang / sprul pa'i sku las chos kyi sku rang bzhin gyis 'a
27'a5(rgyud): gsal ba sems rin po che nges par byung ste/ spros par mdzad do// de nyid sems 'od gsal bsugaso rje chen pos khyod tho de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyam pa
27'a6(rgyud): kyi mtshan nyid bzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnyog pa spangs pa/ nam mkha' ltar gdod nas zhi bar de las thugs rje chen po las mngon par phyogs par gzhog nas/ sems can rgyu khams thams
27'a7(rgyud): rnam par gzigs te/ mi shes pas rga ba po dang / 'tsho bas rnam par khyab pa ste// gzigs nas sgor yang sngags 'dis byang chub kyi sems nye bar skyed pa/ oM hrI d+hi tsi ta A tshal
27'a8(rgyud): byang chub kyi sems skyed pa'i rjes thog nyid la/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis de'i thugs kar sems 'od gsal ba de/ yongs su rdzogs pa'o zla ba 'o dkyila'i kho sbyor byin gyi
27'b1(rgyud): rnabs te/ debazhi na gshegs pa mas cad kyi thugs khar rnam par gzhag go// legs par drug pa'i nam lta' wAr drim meng pa de zlos pams cad spangs pa me long sa bu thur ba skyenas
27'b2(rgyud): gnas te/ byang chub kyi sems chen po la sngags 'di cheng du brjod pa// oM d+hA d+ha ra sI ba sri dza hU~M/ de'i rjes thogs nyid la 'od zer rnam pa sna tshogs pa/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor las rnam par byung ngu
27'b3(rgyud): dbyung nas kyang nus kyi dbyis kyi po brang du zhugs te/ shes bya'i dkyil 'khor thams cad gsal bar byas nas/ sems can thams cad kyi ba'i rtse mo smis te/ rab tu gtogs par byas nas gcis
27'b4(rgyud): 'dres te/ rdo rje'i sku chen po rnams bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs kar rjes su nags nas zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi dbus su rab tu gnas so// de nas bcom ldan 'das dzA rje rnal 'byor
27'b5(rgyud): gyi dbang phyug chen pos// sngags 'dis byin gyis rlabs so// oM ta/ khA badz+ra/ slar yang sngags 'dis spros pa/ oM swa ra badz+rI/ slar yang sngags 'dis skyes so// A~M sa~M har
27'b6(rgyud): drin sa dben ni gshegs pa rnams nad kyis shes rdo rje'i snying po'i 'di cing du brjod pa/ oM dA ne dz+nyA/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rjen la 'byor gyi dang phyuste chen mas / 'dis kyi rgyas nangs
27'b7(rgyud): oM sarba ta thA ga ta dz+nyA na badz+ra hU~M// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs mnyam pa nyid rnyed pas sngags 'dis byin gyis rlabs// oM badz+ra ang mo ka hU~M// de bzhin glu shegs
27'b8(rgyud): pa thams cad rten pa nyid du nye bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs gzigs nas sngags 'dis byin gyis rlabs
28a1(rgyud): spyi 'or dbang bskur bya// yang na gang 'dod rnal 'byor gyi// sbyor ba bsgoms te dbang bskur bya// yang na bdag po'i rnal 'byor gyis// gal te de ni brjod ldan 'gyur// gdugs dang rgyal// 
28a2(rgyud): mtshan bla res sogs// b+haM g+ha ra'i bum pa dang // rnga yab rnam pa sna tshags dang // seng ge'i khri bzang po dang // gser dang dngul gyi dbyug gu dang // rin chen dbyug ga du ma ni// dgyes pa'i dkyil
28a3(rgyud): 'khor nyid du gzhag/ dbang bskur spros pa chen po yis// de ni bstan la gzhag nas su// rnal 'byor ldan pas dbang bskur ro// dbang bskar ji ltar rigs pa yis// gsang ba'i sbyor bas dbang
28a4(rgyud): bskur ro// thog mar sdom pa ldan pa yis// de ni dam tshig 'dzin du 'jug/ 'dir ni nga'i dam tshig bzung // phyigs rab ni rnam pa bzhi// sangs rgyas kun gyi sdom pa ni// sangs rgyas
28a5(rgyud): ye shes rab gsal byed// gdug pa thams cad gsad par byan/ 'dzangs pa ni tsam gyi nor 'phrog bya// lwa ba ngan pa brdzun du smra// srog chags gsod la smra bar bya// gzhan du
28a6(rgyud): bud med mngon 'phrod par// ci bde bar ni khrogs shig bu// gzhan rdzas 'phrog par byed rnams dang // dkon mchog gsum la 'gal byed pa// gsang dang gzhom par bya ba dang // de bzhin khrag
28a7(rgyud): rnams btung bar ru// 'bad pa yis ni thams cad byos// dam tshig rnam pa gsum po yis// de nas yon ni phul nas su// de nas yon ni phul nas su// bla ma la ni gus pa yis// zhabs la
28a8(rgyud): mgo bos nges btud te// rang lus rgyal po'i longs spyod dang // nung ma 'am yang na bu mo dang // bu rnams dang ni bran nyid dang // sring mo sring mo'i bu mo dang // ma dang rang gi gan ma dang // grong dang yul/ 
28b1(rgyud): gyi longs spyod shing rta grong dang glang po dang // rnam par bkra ba'i rta rnams dang // nor gyis gang ba'i grong rnams dang // ba glang ma he ra rnams dang // lug dgod rnams dang gzhan rnams dang / 
28b2(rgyud): rnga mo mdzes pa'i rnga mo ma// gzhan dang gzhan yang gang 'dod pa// ji ltar rigs pas mchod par bya// rims bzhin rang gi slob ma'i tshogs// mgon po mchod nas gshegs su gsol// gang
28b3(rgyud): gzhan rdo rje spun la yang // de nas bsgrub thabs dam pa bslab// srog dang thur sel sbyor ba yis// sems kyis brtan pa nyid du bya// zla ba nya ba lta bur dgang // cha shas dag ni bcu drug kyang // de'i
28b4(rgyud): dbus su rnam bsam pa// gtso chen 'dod pa'i dbang phyug go// mdor sdus nas ni spro bar bya// rdul shugs can gyis rang lus bsam// bdag nyid 'dod pa'i dbang phyug rgya la/ 
28b5(rgyud): 'dod pa'i zil gyis mnan nas su / rnal 'byor can bdag dpal ldan 'grub// lha dang bcas pas phyag 'tshal zhing / nad dang mya ngan 'jigs pa sel// rga dang 'chi ba rnams par
28b6(rgyud): spangs// zla ba tsam bzlas pa yis ni// dpa' bos las kun byed par 'gyur// zhi dang rgyas dang de bzhin dbang // drag shul spyod pa'i rim pa yis// dgug dang dbab pa'i las rnams ni/ 
28b7(rgyud): skad cig tsam zhig bskul ba yis// sngags pas thams cad byed par 'gyur// sngags kyi sbyor bas bsngags bzlos pa'o// 'di ni bcom ldan rnal 'byor gsung // yan lag lA las skyes pa'i
28b8(rgyud): bzung // 'byung po'i nyi ma'i mtshan mo gung // lcags gsum gyis ni bkres byas la// rang gi kha ru gzhug par bya// bdag nyid rnal 'byor ldan pas bzlas// de ni nang par mthong mi 'gyur// ltar
29a1(rgyud): bcas grub pa'i sems can gyis// thams cad rnam pa kun du'o// bskal par gnas shing shes rab che// sten bcos thams cad rab tu mkhas// gzugs dang lang mtsha phun
29a2(rgyud): sum tshogs// rig pa 'dzin pa'i mnga' bdag 'gyur// bcu bzhi'i nyin par shi ba'i// rdol pa'i g.yon gyi rtsib logs ni// sbyor bas bzung ste 'phung 'gre'o// gzugs rnyan lag
29a3(rgyud): pa bzhi pa bya// zhags pa lcags rgyu rtsa gsum mtshan// g.yon par thod pa 'dzin pa'o// rlung gi dkyil 'khor la gnas pa// spyan gsum rnam par rtsigs pa'o// thod pa'i 'phreng ba'i
29a4(rgyud): spyod pan can// rdum ldan lta bu zur chen po pa// 'jig pa chen po'i dur khrod du// rnal 'byor ldan pas de zhig / ste// cho ga ji bzhin mchod par bya// gsang sngags rgyal po zlas
29a5(rgyud): por bya// shi ba yi ni mi dag gi// khrag dang sha dang mar khu yis// de nas lha mo dri 'grub po// mtshan mayang ni lta bar bya// mtshan ma yis ni dngos grub che// dus mi ring
29a6(rgyud): bar bzang po 'thob// dman pas dman pa'i dngos grub ste// khar ma yis ni bar mo'o// mtshan mo med na chung ngu ni// rab tu 'grub par spyad mi dgos// lha mini bzang po dgug par bya// mi dang
29a7(rgyud): mngar ni skul ba yis// de'i skad cig nyid la byed// khrag nyid kyis ni khris pa yi// dbang du bya ba'ang 'di nyid kyis// de bzhin bud med thams cad dgug/ grub pa'i rdzas kyi mang nyid kyis//

29b1(rgyud): gsang pa thams cad ni// cho ga dag dang ldan pas byed// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum rnams rnams dang // yab rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsang ba brgyan gyi dkyis
29b2(rgyud): 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po 'di zhu ba zhus pas/ gang la bzhugs nas rgyal ba kun// yum dang yab rnams de bzhin du// de'i sbyor bas sbyor bdag nyid// sems can rnams ni sdod du mdzod//

29b4(rgyud): bcas pa'i spyan rgyas pas// gsang ba chen po bka' stsal du// glang phyir bdag nyid dkyil 'khor bshad// sems can dag pa'i rdo rje can// bdag nyid gsang ba'i rgyan zhes bya// 
29b5(rgyud): po phyag rgya sngags nyid de/ bdag nyid rigs sngags dam tshig kyang // gang phyir bdag nyid sdom pa ste/ bdag nyid gshed dang 'chang po po// pha dang ma rnams de bzhin no// 
29b6(rgyud): dngos grub bsgrub po las kyi mchog/ bde dang stu/ bsngal khams gsam pa// zhes so nyide nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum dang yab rnams
29b7(rgyud): kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// de'i phyir gsungs cig bcom ldan 'das bde bar gshegs pas gsung du gsol// sangs rgyas byang chub sems kun gyi// phan dang badre ba thob pa'i phyir// ces so//

30a1(rgyud): dang rdo rje las 'di byung ngo // sngon gshad cho ga'i rim pa yis/ dkyil 'khor yang dag bris nas su// de'i dbus su bdag bsam bya// dkar dang dmar dang 'od chen po// sna tshogs
30a2(rgyud): brgyan gyis lus la spras// dmar po'i 'phreng ba gtsug tor can// sna tshogs gos ni legs snams pa// dmar po'i dar gyi bla gos can// phyag bzung g.yon na gril bu ste// / snyems bcas
30a3(rgyud): 'jam bag ldan pa'i zhal// phyag gzhan na ni rdo rje can// snying khar rab tu gsor mdzad pa// pad ma rgyas 'dra'i spyan mnga' ba// zhal kyi dkyil 'khor nyi shar mtshungs// rdo rje seng ge'i khri la
30a4(rgyud): bzhugs// mer po'i gos ni 'chang ba po// dmamA par sdus nas bri bar bya// g.yon du shes rab yongasu bri/ sngon bshad pa'i gzugs can la// g.yas pa'i phyag ni
30a5(rgyud): 'tshed pa'o// lho ru sbyin pa chen mo ni// phyag rab rin/ chen po rtsol ba mo// byang du bzod pa chen mo ni// byams khe'i yan lag 'dzin pa mi// 'dun du brtson 'grus chen mo ni/ 
30a6(rgyud): rdo rje'i lag pa tshe na bzung bkra/ shAr dang lho'i mtshams su ni// bsam gtan pha rol phyini ma bri// bsam gtan phyag can spyan yangs ma// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'od bzang po/ bden
30a7(rgyud): bral du ni 'phel ma bri// rin po che'i brgyan gyis brgyan// nor gyi rgyun ni stong phrag gis sems can mang po bde bar byed// smon lamra br-i bya rlung gi ni// mtshams su yang dag mtshon
30a8(rgyud): par bya// dbyangs snyan pa'i ngag brjod pas// sems can thams cad bskal bar byed// blo gros ldan pas dbang ldan du// thabs kyi ye shes slob pa mo// lag pa dag gis gar byed pa
30b1(rgyud): skyeg dang dga' bas 'khrugs pa bri// dpa' bos shar skor ba bya ba// shes rab pha rol phyin dag ma// ye shes lcags kyu mdzes pa'i phyag/ dmar po'i dmar gyis mngon pararu mdzes
30b2(rgyud): dbang ni nub kyi s+pho ru ni// 'ching ba'i bdag nyid bri bar bya// shin du byi ru dang mtshungs pa// rdo rje lcags sgrog 'dzin pa mo// byang gi sgo ru bri bar bya// stob kyi pha rol phyin mchog ma/ rgyal
30b3(rgyud): ba thams cad mnyes byed pa// dril bu bzang po 'khrol ba'i bdag/ gshin rjer cho 'phrul bri bar bye// 'bar ba'i sngon gyis yang dag 'khrugs// phyag na rdo rje zhags bkra ba// rdo rje'i klog
30b4(rgyud): 'phreng dang mtshungs ma'o// nga'i mdun na shes ldan gyis ga rje 'dod pa'i dbang phyug rgyan pa bri// pad ma ra gA'i 'od gsal ba// mda' dang gzhu ni 'dzin pa'i mchog/ de'i mdun du dkar po bri
30b5(rgyud): zla ba'i 'od 'dra grags chen po// zla ba shar ba'i 'o// mdzes pa// 'dzem bag can la gzhon nu'i gzugs / rdo rje rdzang sgrogs rgyal po ni// dril bu 'khrol ba dang ldan pa/ 
30b6(rgyud): de'i rgyab du bri bar bya// gser dang gur gum dang 'dram// lho'i phyogs su bri bya ba// mkha' 'gro'i dbang phyug dpalnga dang ldan sngon po char srin dang 'dra ba'o// lag nu ril gri
30b7(rgyud): rin chen ldan// de'i mdun na dpa' chen 'dod pa'i// rgyal po bdag nyid chen po bri// 'od zer dmar po lag na gzhu// rin chen 'bar bas rnam par brgyan// de'i lho ru bri bya ba / 
30b8(rgyud): rdo rje rnam par smod pa mchog/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor lhag pa mchog/ rab tu rno ba'i 'bar ba'i phreng // rdo rje dam pa 'dul mdzad pa// rdo rje rin chen mchog gi tog/ kha tog dkar
31a1(rgyud): po cher spo ba// gos sngon rnam par 'chang ba mo// rdo rje Ta ki'i dbang phyug rigs// lag na rin chen dam pa mdzes// de'i rgyab du bri bya ba// rgod dang bcas pa'i bzhin
31a2(rgyud): ras mchog/ nga'i rgyab du bri bya ba// dri'i dbang phyug dbang dbang phyug che// lag na pad ma spring khar 'chang // ban du me me tog rnam 'dra ba// de la mngon par chags pa'i// rdo rje sgo// 
31a3(rgyud): ba spyan 'dzas bri// kar srer bzang po sna tshogs pa// lag na ud pal sngon po bzang // de'i g.yon du dag pa'i// lag na 'khor lo cher dkar bri// sngon pos legs pa'i gnas thab
31a4(rgyud): mchog tu 'dzum pa'i bzhin ras can// lo ma'i rtse mo rgyab du bri// lag na yi de bzhin nor bu mchog/ kha dog sngo sangs dpa' chen po// sems dpa' ldan pa'i thugs can no// de'i lho'i
31a5(rgyud): mA du n+ti// chos 'ching mchog gis bri bar bya// ma tshun phyug ldan rlab dkar ba/ nyim shar k+Sha'i swA/ bu 'dra// nga'i byang du b+hI bar+b+ha/ sdug po bkod pa'i glegs kyi
31a6(rgyud): chen po/ shin du ldang ba'i ma rkang mtshungs// lasa? kyi rdo rje mchog 'dzin pa'o// de'i mdun du bri bya ba// rdo rje skyong ba yid 'phrog bak+ku// gzhad ces rdo rje'i lag pa
31a7(rgyud): can// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnams par brgyan// de'i lho ru bri bya ba// 'phro ba'i rtse mo legs brgyan pa// lhang tsher nag po bung ba 'dra// rdo rje'i gsal shing 'dzin pa'o// rgyas
31a8(rgyud): du rdo rje 'ching ba bri// lag pa yang dag sbyar sngams pa// rin chen kun gyi 'od dag cing // 'dzum bcas mchog tu ngo mtshar ba// 'o khyed g.yon du bri bar bya// lag na 'khor lo'i
31b1(rgyud): 'gal me'i 'khor lo can// legs o dar la bab pa'o// rab rgyas pad ma lca bu'i zhal// de nasna sgo'i cha dag du// sharA du rdo rje mi bayo ba// lho'i sgo ru rdo rje me// lag na rdo rje
31b2(rgyud): lcags kyu che// lag na rdo rje zhags pa 'bar// nub du rlung ni sngon po ste// rdo rje legs spogs 'dzin pa'o// lus ngan du ni chu bris te// zhugs pa ldan pa'i dril bu 'dzin// de nas/ 
31b3(rgyud): sbyor ldan 'ongs nas su// dkyil 'khor gyi ni sha raM du br-ig/ shar du mnga'i mtshon cha lags// rab dmar pad ma ltar 'bar ba// lho ru me tog chen po can// sngon po drabang phyug rdo rje ma

37b3(rgyud): rgya 'ang de'ang mtshungs// rin chen gyi'ang rin chen che// rin chen mag 'od gsal la// de bzhin dri dang ldan pa ni// sgrub pa pos yos 'grub par 'gyur// de la sogs pa'i dpe ba yis// de las/ 
37b4(rgyud): pas dpe' yis// lha gzhan dag kyang rig par bya/ dam 'khor ram ni dam tshig kyang // sgom pas myur du'agrub par 'gyur// snying po snying dang phyag rgya dang // rigs sngags
37b5(rgyud): kyi'ang sbyor ba yis// de rnams kyi'ang de nyid nas/ snyoms ma myur du nges par 'grub// 'di ni bcom ldan rdo rje can// gsang ba'i brgyan dag dam pas gsungs
37b6(rgyud): phyag rgya bzhi'i mtshan gyi mchog/ phyag rgya thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// zhes so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yab dang yum de rnams kyis gsol ba// myur du sbyor ba
37b7(rgyud): mchog bsgrubs pas// sgrub pa pos ni ji ltar 'grub de/ de dag thams cad myur du gsungs// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang bdag gis// snying po sngags dang phyag rgya dang // rig sa sngags
37b8(rgyud): dag ni lo ga sa par 'grub/ btsun mo mchog gi gnas dbang phyug/ dpa' bo chen pos gsung du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang pos// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
38a1(rgyud): kyi gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ba rnam par sbyangs pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yab dang yum rnams kyi zhu ba'i tshig rdo rje 'di
38a2(rgyud): nyid kyi sku dang // gsung dang thugs rnams las phyung ngo // lha rnams kyi snying ni snying po dang // sngags dang phyag rgya de bzhin du// dkyil 'khor gyi ni legs par gshad// ji ltar sngon du kha dog sogs
38a3(rgyud): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis slar yang 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis gsung du gsol// sems can rnams la phan bde'i phyir// rnal 'byor ma'i phyag rgya dang // 
38a4(rgyud): mtshan ma la sogs dam pa rnams// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang // rdo rje dam par gsor bar mdzad// lag pa'i dmatshan ma bka' stsal pa// gang gis lha rnams mchod 'gyur ba/ 
38a5(rgyud): lag pa zla ba nyi ma ru// mkhas pa yis ni bri bar byan/ shes rab thabs kyi sa bon ni// rnal 'byor can gyis rtag tu s+ho// slar yang sdud pa'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje pad ma rnams gas/ 
38a6(rgyud): bya// de nas shes rab pha rol phyin// sor mo'i rtse mor bgod par bya// de nyid sbyor bas skus nas su// phan tshun nges par sbyar bar bya// rdo rje pad ma mnyam sbyor bas// bde ba myangs pas 'grub par 'gyur
38a7(rgyud): 'ching ba chen pos bcings nas su// lha mo'i sa bon gyis mtshan pa'i// gsang sngags rgyal po sngags pas ni// yang dang yang du byin gyis rlab// bcings te 'od ldan rnam pa gnyis// rkyang nas rtse mo / 
38a8(rgyud): sbyar bar bya// de 'di snying po zhes bya'o// gnyis pa grags pa ldan pa yin// snying po yis ni mtshan byas nas// rims kyis snying kar bskor bar bya// rdo rje mnyam par sbyar bya te// der ni bcings
38b1(rgyud): pa bzhug par bya// 'di ni dam tshig zhes bya ste// dam tshig ma lus bsgrub par byed// 'di yis lha mo mtha' yas zhal// thams cad du ni nges par 'grub// de nyid sngags pa lta bur sbyar// las kun byed pa'i
38b2(rgyud): mchog du 'gyur// rdo rje gnyis ni pad ma yis// sbyor ba rtag tu mchod du rmad// de las phyi rol bskums pa ni// gsam pa'u ni 'gyur ba yin// snying dga' byed pa zhes byar brjod// rdo rje gnyis pa de bzhin
38b3(rgyud): sbyar// dam tshig dag byed nyid du 'gyur// de nyid kun gyi 'byung gnas gsal// chen po'i las ni byed par 'gyur// de nyid mdzad spur sbyar ba rdzing // phyag rgya bdag nyid chen por 'gyur// de nyid chu skyes
38b4(rgyud): rnam par ru// snying khar gzhag pa snying po mchog/ de/ bzhin rdo rje mnyam sbyor ba// dam tshig bdag nyid ched du/ 'gyur// snying khar kun sdigs sbyor ba yis// rab rgyas pa'i bzhin
38b5(rgyud): ras mchog/ mnyes par byed pa thams cad kyang // snying gi dkyil 'khor nyid du bzung // 'di ni dam tshig dngos grub che// bdag nyid chen pos bslab par bya// las kyi
38b6(rgyud): sems pa yis/ ka las rnams thams cad rab bsgrub byed// dbab dang 'khor ba nyid du ni// gar byed chen po de bzhin du// de bzhini thal mo sbyar nas su// snying khar gzhag pa snying por
38b7(rgyud): bshad// spyi bor bskor ba byas pa ni// dam tshig zhes bya bdag nyid che// steng du sdigs pa las ni 'gyur// mchod pa ma lus rab bsgrub byed// snying po la sogs 'og tu bzung // chos la sogs par
38b8(rgyud): yongasu brtag/ de nyid rkyang ste snying po zhes// su legs par bshad// bskor ba dam tshig zhes bya ste// las kyang thams cad de bzhin no// de nas thal mo rdo rje gnyis// steng sgreng snying po
39a1(rgyud): la sngags yongasu rtag/ sngon bshad lha mo thams cad kyi/ gsang sngags rig pas shes par bya/ gnyis su byas la g.yas min pas// bsgrub bya'i 'grin la bzung nas su// mngon par
39a2(rgyud): phyogs te bzhag par bya// gzugs kyi snying po chos che'o// de nyid kha'i phyogs gzhag pa// skra'i snying po'i yid 'phrog pa'o// de nyid cung zad bskums nas su// lce'i rnam pas kha ru gzhag/ 
39a3(rgyud): rero myang ba'i sbyor ba yis// snying khar legs sbyar sbyor bdag gis// de nyid la'ang rnam pa bzhi// phyag rgya sngags pas shes par bya// ro 'phrog pa'i las rnams so// de ni gnyis su byas nas sa
39a4(rgyud): g.yas pa 'o ma ni g.yon pa yis// snying khar li gso sbyar sbyor bdag gis// ring ba'i phyag rgya ngo mtshar che// da 'di yis chos dang dam tshig dang // las kyang rab ste skye ba yin// 
39a5(rgyud): cho ga shes pas rnal 'byor sbyar// reg pas 'bebs po'i mchog yin no// de bzhin sbyar ba so sor bya// gsu ba rkyed par gzhag par bya// g.yas pa kha'i phyogs su gzhag/ 
39a6(rgyud): khro ba'i tshul gyis de bzhin du// 'di ni gzhang ldan zhes bya ba'i// phyag rgya mchog du rmad 'byung ngo // de las bkrol te snga ma bzhin/ rkyed pa ru ni legs par gzhag/ de las lengs te sngar
39a7(rgyud): yang khar// mkhas pas dal gyis skyong bar bya// de gnyis snying khar yongs su sbyar// snyoms par 'dud dang 'gyed par byed// ji srid spyi bor btugs pa yis// chos dang la sogs kun du
39a8(rgyud): 'gyur// snying po la sogs sngags rim pas// phyag rgya 'di yis brgyas btab no// dngos grub thams cad thob 'gyur te// rdo rje sems dpa'i dka' bzhin no// thal mo mnyam par legs par
39b1(rgyud): legs par sbyar// g.yon pa'i steng du de bzhin gzhag/ de dag snying khar bsgreng bar bya// de ni phan tshun shes rab yin// sngags pa chen pos sbyor bar bya// gzhan ni sbyor bas rnam par spo// 
39b2(rgyud): 'di ni chos kyi pha rol du// 'gro ba'i chos kyi mchog tu bshad// de bzhin thal mo mnyam por sbyor// snying khar g.yon par gzhag par bya// 'od ldan rdo rje'i gdong pa dang // mdor skus nas
39b3(rgyud): ni sbyar nas su// g.yas pa mthur du 'phyang bar bya// de bzhin steng bstan mchog sbyin no// me tog snyim pa yang dag sbyar// rdo rje gnyis ni dbus su gzhag/ bzod pa gnyis po de la sbyar// 
39b4(rgyud): de ni steng du legs par bzhag/ da ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// yid bzhin rgyal po'i 'bras bur ster// de ni skyer dpas so sor bya// g.yon pa'i snying khar yongasu gzhag// g.yas pa
39b5(rgyud): sngo ba'i sbyor ba yis// yongs su zhing bskor nas su// g.yas pa ru ni gzhag par bya// rdo rje thal mo rkyang nas su// rdo rje'i steng du mdzes ma ste// phyi rol bskum pa'i skyo ba yis// 
39b6(rgyud): de'i steng du gdong pa gzhag// phyag rgya 'di ni phyag rgya che// brtson 'grus pha rol phyin dge ma'o// de bzhin lag pa steng du sbyar// rtsibs mchog rin chen ma ru 'gyur// lhag ma'i bya ba de nyid kyis
39b7(rgyud): de bzhin gzhag cing bsam par bya// sbyor ba de yis bcing ba ru// sngags shes rtso bo sngags pas bya// rdo rje la thal mo mnyam par sbyar// khro bo rdo rje'i sbyor ba yis// stor khar blo gros ldan pas bzang
39b8(rgyud): de ni lpags kyi nam pa yis// snying khor blo gros ldan pas bzung / de ni lcags kyu'i rnam pa yis// lhas nas lus can 'gugs por byed// de nas so rims so rnams/ hud zad bsdol te brkyang ba de/ 
40a1(rgyud): rdo rje 'che ba lta bur snang // kha sbyar sgrol byed ngo mtshar che/ rgya 'di rnams kyi rgyus btab pa// las rnams thams cad byed par 'gyur// de las thal mor byas nas su// gzi brjid rdo rje de
40a2(rgyud): bzhin no// de bzhin lcags kyus dbug pa s+ho// de'i mtha' gdong zhags pa'o// sog le'i thal mo nges par ni// 'dir ni thod pa nyid du 'gyur// 'di ni gnyis pa nyid yin te// lus kun gyi ni dam
40a3(rgyud): ba bsgrub// de bzhin bcing ba legs bcings nas// rab tu smyon pabarkyang bar bya// g.yas pa steng du byas nas su// gsang ba lta bur btsang bar bya// 'di ni rdo rje mdung thung ste// srin po thams cad phye
40a4(rgyud): mar byed// 'dir ni de bzhin thod pa dang // zhags/ pa ljags kyu nyid dang yang // sog le dang ni gri thung gi/ rdo rje thal mo'i tshogs bcas dang // rdo rje la mo so sor bya// lag pa
40a5(rgyud): g.yas pa steng du ni// rin chen lta bur byas la bzung sor mo thams cad spro bar bya// g.yon pa'ang de bzhin sgra bar bya// thal mo sbreng ste shes rab dang // las kyi rdo rje rtse mo sbyar
40a6(rgyud): 'di ni las rnams thams cad kyi// sna tshogs las mchog bsgrub par byed// de bzhin dgug dang zhags pa dang // thod pa rdo rje nyid yin no// de las thal mo thod pa ni// phyag rgya'i dbus su bu ga ni
40a7(rgyud): sngon ma can zhes legs bshad de// 'di ni rdo rje ngo mtshar che// zhags pa lcags kyu de bzhin du// slob dpon blo gros ldan pas shes// gzungs rnams dag ni thams cad kyi// sngar bshad pa
40a8(rgyud): phyag rgya nyid// thod pa rdo rje'ang shes par bya// phan tshun gcig la gcig tu ni// thams cad gzungs kyi phyag rgya ru// dkyil 'khor du ni rab tu bsgrags// 'di rnams sbyor ba ji lta bar/ 
40b1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor bzhi ni rtag par ru// rdo rje slob dpon gyis bya ste// phyag na rdo rje'i bka' bzhin no// 'di ni bcom ldan rdo rje gsung // kun bzang bdag nyid chen po pa// sems can kun mchog las
40b2(rgyud): kyi mchog/ sangs rgyas mchog rtso mnga' bdag che// zhes so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang po yang // 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ye shes rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la
40b3(rgyud): snyoms par zhugs nas// de dag thams cad la yang dang yang du gzigs te// sems can khams thams cad brtson 'grus zhan po// spro ba dman pa dman pa la mos par gzigs nas/ de rnams
40b4(rgyud): la bka' sgo bar dam pa'i ma mo rnams kyis shod/ rang rang gi ni sgrub sna tshogs// de nas de bzhin legs tshim nas// rdo rje can la gsol ba ni// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par
40b5(rgyud): rdo rje dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de'i steng du rdo rje che rdo rje la ni dngos po mchog/ nyi ma gser mdog dang mtshungs par// gsang sngags shes pas de sgom bya// rang gi lus las spros
40b6(rgyud): nas su// rang gi rnam par bsam par bya// de nas sngags bdag 'grub par 'gyur// sngags kyi de nyid bdag po cher// kun du 'gro ba sna tshogs che// rdo rje sems dpa' 'dra ba gzhan// gnyis bya de nyid
40b7(rgyud): bsgom pa ni// dkyil 'khor pad ma las byung ba// dmar po'i gose la gze brjid che// 'bar ba dag la me dang mtshungs// rang las sgro bya thams cad du// 'jig rten dbang phyug lta bur 'gyur// dkyil
40b8(rgyud): 'khor dbang chen bzhag par bya// dkyil 'khor la ni cher dge mo// dang po lha mo drod dang ldan// rang gi lus la nges par khyab// bsdus nas bdag dang 'dra ba'i bdag// yid bzhin nor bu'i snang bar
41a1(rgyud): 'gyur// rlung gi dkyil 'khor dbus son par// 'gro ba'i sgo rten lha mo ni// rang lus lus ldan thams cad du// ldeng khu dang ni ljang ser ma// las kun bsgrub pa'i dam pa'i// rdo rje 'dzin pa
41a2(rgyud): dpal ljon 'gyur// ma mo bzhi dang yang dag ldan// shes rab ye shes dam pa gnas// dkyil 'khor kun gyi dam par ru// mkhas pa yis ni bsgom par bya// kun gyi bdag po dpal dang ldan// kun bzang mnga' bdag
41a3(rgyud): chen po ni// bsam gtan dkyil 'khor sbyor ba yis// thams cad nyid na bsgrub par bya// chos kyi yi ge yang dag sbyar// lha mni bdag por bdag 'gyur ro// zhes bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang pos bka' stsal to// 
41a4(rgyud): gsang ba brgyan gyi rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po las// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yab dang // 'khor dang bcas pa rnams slar yang 'dus par gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kun
41a5(rgyud): du bzang po la dbyangs kyi rgyal po 'dis gsol ba btab pa// thos cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes che// mkha' la rlung ltar cher gshegs pa/ yab kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes bzang // kun mchog dam pas gsung du
41a6(rgyud): gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang pos de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyal po mchog/ rdo rje dpal zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// ye shes chen po'i phyag rgya dang // dkyis
41a7(rgyud): 'khor 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje rgyas pa las nges par phyung ngo // dbus su nyi ma chen po ni// hUM yig sbyor bas bsam par bya// sor mo kun gyi rtse gnas te// sa bon lnga'i yab dgod bya// tshogs
41a8(rgyud): kyi nang ni thams cad du// yi ge thams cad rnam par bsam// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dag la ni// bzang po thams cad rnam bsam bya// 'khor lo chen po'i phyag rgya'i tshul// lag pa g.yon par bsam par bya// 
41b1(rgyud): de'i dbus su shes rab che// de bzhin gzhan yang dgod par bya// de nyid spro ba'i de nyid ni// gsang sngags 'di yis sbyar bar bya// oM pra dz+nyA ba ya ma ya yo gau hU~M aM// de nas phan tshun sbyar nas// rdo rje thal
41b2(rgyud): po rab tu gnas// rdo rje sngams pas byas nas su// rdo rje skams par rnam par bsam// de nas shes rab che sbeng ste// rtse mo cung zad sdums par bya// 'dod pa'i dbang phyug snying por 'gyur// snying khar gnag na sa
41b3(rgyud): po 'grub// de nyid sdigs pa'i sbyor ba yis// las kyi mchog du 'gyur ba yin// de nyid snying khar sdams pa ni// phyag rgya chen po zhes su grags// thams cad kyis kyang mdor sdus pa'i// las rnams thams
41b4(rgyud): cad rab sgrub byed// de bzhin legs par bcing bar byed// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin pa gnyis// phyi'i rgyab du skums par bya// mkha' 'gro'i dbang phyug snying dga' ba'o// shes rab de ni de bzhin sbyor
41b5(rgyud): dam tshig zhes par rab tu grags// lha ma rnam pa spro bar/ bya// las kyi gnas 'khod chen por grags// shes rab dag ni zlum tshul gyis// dri'i dbang phyug rab dges ma'o// bzod dang brtson 'grus
41b6(rgyud): gdong ba gnyis// lo ma'i tshul du rkyang bar bya// dam tshig grub pa ster bar gshad// 'di las rtse mo rnam bye ma// las kun byed pa zhes bshad de// ra ba thams cad rdzogs par byed// de nyid rtse mo snying khar sbyar da
41b7(rgyud): bdag nyid chen po'i phyag rgya mchog// rgyal po mchog lha'i rgyal po ru// 'di yis myur du 'grub par 'gyur// rdo rje sdams pas shes rab 'od// dril bu'i rnam pa snying po mchog/ bzod dang brtson 'grus gdong
41b8(rgyud): sbyar ba// dam tshig mnyam pa nyid du gnas// cung zad gdod pa skum par bya// las byed pa'i mchog tu 'gyur// gdod pa legs par rkyang nas su// steng du shes rab rtse mo gcig/ 'di ni chen por shes bya ste//

42a2(rgyud): bye ste rin po che// 'di ni dam tshig ldan pa'i mchog/ de gnyis de bzhin rnam par bzhag/ sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin dge dag/ rang rkyang zhi bzhi sems dpa'i// las rnams thams cad byed par bshad// de bzhin tshul

42a6(rgyud): brkyang nas ni// rna ba'i rtsa bar dgug par bya// 'di ni las byed shes bya ste// sangs rgyas byang chub rab bsgrub byed// rdo rje sems dpa' rkyang nas su// snying khar 'khor lo'i tshul bya ba// g.yas pa'i rtse
42a7(rgyud): mor lcags kyur bya// sbyin pa sbyin pa'i pha rol son// de bzhin bcings la legs snga mas bya// gnyi ka de bzhin lcags kyu ste// de bzhin 'og ma bcug nas su// snying khar gzhag pa las rjes 'breng // de nyid dgug

42b1(rgyud): rdo rje chos su bshad pa ste// kha ru g.yo bar byed pa mchog/ las rnams rnam par tshim zhes bya// las kun byed pa'i dam pa ste// lag pa bcings pa las bkrol te// shes rab 'dzed du rab tu rtags// 'di
42b2(rgyud): ni dam tshig cher 'dzes pa// de phyir da ltar chos mdzod do// g.yas pas rab tu bsgribs pa ni// mi snang 'dzad de de des legs// rin chen ldan pas pad ma'i gdong // snying khar gzhag pa snying por 'gyur//

42b7(rgyud): ma'i rnam pa mchog du bya// ster byed pa ni mig ltar bya// snying khar gzhag pas kun mchog 'grub// de nyid mig gzhag las yin no// gzhad pas chos te dam pa'i chos// dam tshig gsang ba'i mig yin
42b8(rgyud): pad ma'i 'dzod la rab tu gnas// thal mo yang dag sbyar ba ni// snying po'i mchog du rmad 'byung ba'o// kha ni nung bzang phye ba ste// dam smyig mchog gi mchog yin no// snying khar shin du gsal phye ba// ma lus las
43a1(rgyud): ni rab tu bsgrub// rdo rje'i nang du pad ma ni// chos steng mchog du rmad 'byung ba'o// 'di rnams kyi ni myur 'grub ste// sngags pas sngags kyis bskul bas so// de bzhin 'ching ba legs
